## HOW TO START A NEW SESSION

1. Run `th` in Terminal — reads CLAUDE.md and copies to clipboard
2. Open claude.ai → New conversation
3. Paste the opener below, fill in CURRENT ISSUE from clipboard

```
PROJECT: Treehouse Finds — Zen-Forged/treehouse-treasure-search — app.kentuckytreehouse.com
STACK: Next.js 14 App Router · TypeScript · Tailwind · Framer Motion · Anthropic SDK · Supabase · SerpAPI · Vercel
Filesystem MCP is connected at /Users/davidbutler/Projects/treehouse-treasure-search
Read CLAUDE.md, CONTEXT.md, and docs/DECISION_GATE.md. Then run the session opening standup from MASTER_PROMPT.md.

CURRENT ISSUE:
[paste here]
```

## HOW TO END A SESSION

Run `/session-close` — replaces the old `thc` alias with the full close protocol (tombstoning, memory updates, commit + push, PR creation).

## TERMINAL COMMAND FORMATTING CONVENTION
> When Claude surfaces multiple terminal commands to run in sequence, each goes in its own fenced block. This lets David copy one at a time and verify each before running the next.

**Do this:**

```bash
npm run build 2>&1 | tail -30
```

```bash
git add -A && git commit -m "..." && git push
```

**Not this** (chained separate commands in one block that invite blind paste):

```bash
npm run build 2>&1 | tail -30
git add -A && git commit -m "..." && git push
```

Exception: a single chained command with `&&` stays in one block — that's one atomic action by design.

Worktree rebased onto origin/main. Then Layer 2 kickoff per session-148 close opener.

### Pre-work — Worktree drift + Vercel transient build error

**NEW pattern observed (single firing — Tech Rule candidate on 2nd firing): "Worktree drift detection on session-open when stale CLAUDE.md auto-loaded."** When user's session count conflicts with what's in auto-loaded CLAUDE.md / git log, the canonical authority is `git log origin/main` + `gh pr list --search "Session N"` — checking both surfaces drift in 1-2 round trips. Sub-pattern of `feedback_visibility_tools_first` extended to session-state verification.

**NEW pattern observed (single firing — Tech Rule candidate on 2nd firing): "Vercel transient build error diagnosed via Vercel MCP list_deployments without patching."** Production deploy of merge commit `8628c46` failed at git-clone with HTTP 500 from GitHub; preview deploy of same content (`7c52243`, parent of the merge) succeeded 20 seconds earlier. Diagnosis: transient flake on Vercel ↔ GitHub side, not a build problem. Round-0 escalation per `feedback_cap_speculative_patching_at_3_rounds` — visibility tools first, correct action was retry, not code change. Sub-pattern of `feedback_visibility_tools_first` extended to platform-level flakes.

### Audit-first per `feedback_visibility_tools_first` + cost-shape triage per `feedback_triage_cost_shape_before_design_pass` (✅ Promoted)

Explore-agent dispatch against `components/ShareSheet.tsx` (2090 LOC, 81 v1 refs — heaviest remaining v1 surface) with structured 5-section query: primitive clusters / API surfaces / cross-surface generalization signals / starter primitive set / sequencing risks. Agent localized 3 highest-ROI primitive clusters: **BottomSheet** (scrim + handle + TopBar, duplicated 3× verbatim across BoothShareBody + MallShareBody + FindShareBody) / **SlimHeader** (3 near-identical entity-discriminated variants) / **ChannelGrid** (9+ render sites + stateful CopyLinkTile).

**3 cost shapes for Layer 2 kickoff**: **A** surgical (extract 2-3 highest-ROI primitives + validate adoption on one consumer) / **B** systematic (full ~9 primitive set in isolation, adopt across top-debt consumers) / **C** parallel-track (Layer 2 + ShareSheet v2 sub-arc together — `<Sheet>` extracted as byproduct of ShareSheet migration). **David: "Shape A"**. **First-consumer triage**: admin/page.tsx (56 violations) / ShareSheet.tsx (33 violations + folds into ShareSheet v2 sub-arc) / find/[id]/page.tsx (22). My lean + David's call: **ShareSheet** — heaviest v1 surface + 3 primitive consumers in single file + extracting `<Sheet>` while shipping the migration kills two birds in one arc.

### Implementation arcs (5 commits sequenced smallest→largest per `feedback_smallest_to_largest_commit_sequencing` — 5 firings this session, cumulative ~263+)

- **2.1 lib/tokens.ts MOTION_BOTTOM_SHEET_* tokens** (`6d0e395`, +11/−0). Additive — 3 new constants (MOTION_BOTTOM_SHEET_EASE / *_BACKDROP_DURATION / *_SHEET_DURATION) added alongside existing MOTION_EASE_OUT + MOTION_SHARED_ELEMENT_* family. Values mirror the inline EASE + 0.22 + 0.34 currently duplicated 3× inside ShareSheet body components. Named separately so future bottom-sheet motion can diverge without ambiguity (precedent: MOTION_SHARED_ELEMENT_EASE deliberately diverges from MOTION_EASE_OUT despite both being ease-curves, session 78).
- **2.2 `<BottomSheet>` primitive + /ui-test smoke route** (`0bf274e`, +388/−0). First Layer 2 primitive. Modal scrim + bottom-sheet container + handle pill + TopBar (back + close). API: `open` / `onClose` / `ariaLabel` / `showBack?` / `onBack?` / `closeDisabled?` / `children`. v1 → v2 token migration applied at extraction: `v1.paperCream → v2.bg.main`; `v1.inkFaint → v2.text.muted` (handle); `v1.inkHairline → v2.border.light` (button border); `v1.inkMid → v2.text.secondary` (glyph stroke); `rgba(255,255,255,0.5) → v2.surface.card` (button bg — frosted-glass retire per session 132). PRESERVED as canonical modal vocabulary (NOT frosted-glass per session 146 Arc 7.4.2 precedent): backdrop `rgba(30,20,10,0.38)` (modal scrim); sheet `boxShadow rgba(30,20,10,0.28)` (sheet-rise elevation). Body scroll lock lives inside the primitive (was duplicated 3× across ShareSheet). Intrinsic sizing PRESERVED verbatim from session 41+135 (handle 44×4, TopBar 36px, max-width 430px, max-height 92vh, sheet radius 20px). `/ui-test` smoke route mirrors testbed-first precedent — **5th cumulative firing of `feedback_testbed_first_for_ai_unknowns`** (postcard-test 107 + search-bar-test 102 + geolocation-test 118 + vendors-test 125 + ui-test 149); pattern now generalizes beyond AI-unknowns to "primitive isolation."
- **2.3 `<SlimHeader>` primitive + ui-test consumer** (`5ccdb94`, +286/−0). Second Layer 2 primitive. Entity-discriminated context block — single primitive serves all 3 entity tiers via optional rows. API: `title` / `titleClamp?` / `boothPill?` / `contextLabel?` / `addressLine?`. Variants map as: Booth (title + pill + mall + addr) / Mall (title + no pill + city + addr) / Find (title + titleClamp=2 + pill + vendor + mallContext). v1 → v2 + font migration: FONT_LORA → FONT_CORMORANT (title + context label); FONT_SYS → FONT_INTER (pill + address). **Bug fix at extraction**: Find variant's previous lineHeight 1.15 was under the 1.3 Lora descender floor (clamped + overflow:hidden = clipping risk on line 2 descenders). Primitive raises clamped titles to 1.3 automatically per `feedback_lora_lineheight_minimum_for_clamp` (✅ Promoted session 107; ~13 cumulative firings post-promotion). Section divider renders unconditionally so sheet body has consistent boundary.
- **2.4 `<ChannelGrid>` primitive + ui-test consumer** (`c8d448a`, +244/−0). Third Layer 2 primitive. 3-column share-channel tile grid with **discriminated tile array**: `{kind: "channel"; icon; label; onClick}` or `{kind: "copy"; url; onTap; onCopySuccess}`. Copy state lives INSIDE the primitive (clipboard.writeText + 1600ms checkmark feedback + cleanup-on-unmount timeout). Consumers no longer manage parallel useState/useRef per copy tile. v1 → v2 + font migration: FONT_LORA → FONT_CORMORANT (label); `v1.green → v2.accent.green` (copied-state); `rgba(255,255,255,0.4) → v2.surface.card` (tile bg — frosted-glass retire). Grid is column-count-agnostic via `gridTemplateColumns: repeat(tiles.length, 1fr)`.
- **2.5 ShareSheet body adoption (coupled v1 → v2 migration + primitive swap)** (`e332d0a`, +477/−1344, **−867 net delete** — largest single-commit delete since session 115 /login/email retirement). 3 entity body components (Booth + Mall + Find) adopt the 3 primitives from Layer 2.2–2.4 AND the remaining inline screens (EmailScreen + SentBody + QrScreen × 3) migrate v1 → v2 tokens + Lora → Cormorant + Inter. Retired from ShareSheet (now owned by Layer 2 primitives): 3× motion.div backdrop + sheet + handle pill blocks; 3× useEffect body-scroll-lock; TopBar function + ArrowLeftGlyph + CloseGlyph; 3× SlimHeader variants; ChannelTile function; CopyLinkTile function + internal state. Retained as internal shared helpers (single consumer; promote on 2nd surfacing): QrDisplay; ShareViaEyebrow; FooterDisclaimer. v1 → v2 token + font migration applied across remaining screens: `v1.inkPrimary → v2.text.primary`; `v1.inkMid → v2.text.secondary`; `v1.inkMuted → v2.text.muted`; `v1.inkFaint → v2.text.muted` (collapse); `v1.inkHairline → v2.border.light`; `v1.inkWash → v2.surface.card` (session 146 canonical — **4th cumulative firing**); `v1.postit → v2.surface.card` (session 147 canonical for QrDisplay); `v1.green → v2.accent.green`; `v1.redBg → v2.surface.error`; `v1.redBorder → v2.border.error`; `v1.red → v2.accent.red`; `v1.inkFaint dashed → v2.border.medium` (Share-again button per Arc 7.3.4 dropzone-border precedent); `rgba(30,77,43,0.10) → v2.accent.greenSoft` (Sent success bubble bg — session 146 /login ActionCard icon-wash pattern); `"#f5ecd8" cream → v2.surface.card` (Send button text + PaperAirplaneIcon stroke + Spinner borderTopColor — cream-on-saturated-color canonical session 143); FONT_LORA → FONT_CORMORANT; FONT_SYS → FONT_INTER. **6-axis verification grep PASSES** — zero remaining inline v1.*, FONT_LORA, FONT_SYS, rgba(255,255,255,0.4), rgba(255,255,255,0.5), or any v1 chrome literals in ShareSheet. PRESERVED as canonical brand-presentational utility (NOT chrome): QR logo halo `#ffffff` + boxShadow `0 0 0 4px #ffffff`; Spinner border `rgba(245,236,216,0.35)` cream translucency on saturated green (canonical spinner-on-green vocabulary). Preserved verbatim across migration: /api/share-booth backend + Q-011 4-client-audited email template + Q-008 auth modes + all 4 EmailStatus states + 7 R3 analytics events + errorCopyFor copy table + screen state machine.

### NEW patterns observed (single firings, all Tech Rule candidates on 2nd firing)

1. **"Worktree drift detection on session-open when stale CLAUDE.md auto-loaded"** — sub-pattern of `feedback_visibility_tools_first` extended to session-state verification. Canonical authority is `git log origin/main` + `gh pr list --search`.
2. **"Vercel transient build error diagnosed via Vercel MCP list_deployments without patching"** — sub-pattern of `feedback_visibility_tools_first` extended to platform-level flakes. Preview-vs-production comparison localizes whether it's a code problem in 1 round-trip.
3. **"Layer 2 primitive extraction with coupled adoption ships v1 surface to v2-pure end-to-end"** — extracting a primitive forces the adoption commit to handle both primitive swap AND any pending token migration in the consumer; net effect is the v1 surface crosses to v2-pure as a byproduct of the primitive extraction. Generalizes to any future Layer 2 primitive that has remaining v1 consumers.
4. **"Recursive design-pass discipline applies even when user asks for scoping not implementation"** — Review Board ask was framed as "when to implement?" Response ran reference + cost shapes + frozen decisions + sequencing inline. Mid-conversation design pass is the right shape because the answer to "when" depends on the cost-shape pick.

- **RESOLVED (session 110→134): Home masonry right-column slide-down on entrance** ✅ closed via session-134 commit `5d70c75`. Bug class was a two-paint sequence: column-2 marginTop initialized at SKELETON_OFFSET (70, useState init guess correct for skeleton's 4:5 photo-only tile) → useEffect runs AFTER browser paints → measure() updates state to actual ~100–120px (real tile = 4:5 photo + relative-timestamp "below" row + polaroid mat padding) → second paint snaps to new offset. Browser's snap between two paints reads as a slide-down animation even though no CSS transition is set. Single useEffect → useLayoutEffect swap lands the measurement in the first paint; ResizeObserver registration unchanged (first tile's height can still shift post-mount). 24-session-deep carry retires.

- **/my-shelf admin scroll-restore** ✅ — **resolved session 86** in `0c53fb3` (refuse-to-write-0 fix) + `e311dce` (cleanup). Bug: Next.js App Router scroll-to-top fired real scroll events on outbound navigation; the scroll listener wrote 0 to storage, clobbering the user's good scroll position. Fix: write-side filter (`if (rounded <= 0) return`). Confirmed via iPhone QA. **Phase 3 scroll-restore now closed end-to-end across all 3 surfaces.** Session 85's structural patches (BFCache pageshow handler, popstate, useSearchParams reactivity, dual-write storage, retry-scrollTo loop) stay in place as harmless defensive code; aggressive revert is a follow-up under extended QA.
